      // Legacy model\n}\n```\n\n**Mail Loading Patterns** (`/app/src/mail/model/MailUtils.ts`, lines 397-408):\n\nThe `loadMailDetails()` function handles three scenarios:\n\n```typescript\nexport async function loadMailDetails(entityClient: EntityClient, mail: Mail): Promise<MailWrapper> {\n  if (isLegacyMail(mail)) {\n    // Legacy: Load MailBody directly via mail.body reference\n    return entityClient.load(MailBodyTypeRef, neverNull(mail.body))\n      .then((b) => MailWrapper.body(mail, b))\n  } else if (isDetailsDraft(mail)) {\n    // New model: Load MailDetailsDraft for draft emails\n    return entityClient.load(MailDetailsDraftTypeRef, neverNull(mail.mailDetailsDraft))\n      .then((d) => MailWrapper.details(mail, d.details))\n  } else {\n    // New model: Load MailDetailsBlob for received/sent emails\n    const mailDetailsId = neverNull(mail.mailDetails)\n    return entityClient\n      .loadMultiple(MailDetailsBlobTypeRef, listIdPart(mailDetailsId), [elementIdPart(mailDetailsId)])\n      .then((d) => MailWrapper.details(mail, d[0].details))\n  }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 2. Session Key Management and Storage\n\n**Key Concepts:**\n\nSession keys are stored in multiple locations depending on the permission model:\n\n### Legacy Permission Model (Pre-Blob Migration)\n- **_ownerEncSessionKey**: Encrypted with the owning group's key\n- **Location**: On the Mail entity itself\n- **Decryption**: `decryptKey(ownerGroupKey, _ownerEncSessionKey)`\n\n### New Permission Model (Bucket-based)\n- **bucketKey**: An aggregate containing encrypted session keys for multiple entities\n- **BucketKey structure** (`/app/src/api/entities/sys/TypeRefs.ts`, lines 454-463):\n\n```typescript\nexport type BucketKey = {\n  _type: TypeRef<BucketKey>;\n  _id: Id;\n  groupEncBucketKey: null | Uint8Array;     // Encrypted with group key\n  pubEncBucketKey: null | Uint8Array;       // Encrypted with public key\n  bucketEncSessionKeys: InstanceSessionKey[];  // Array of instance session keys\n  keyGroup: null | Id;                      // Group used for encryption\n}\n```\n\n### InstanceSessionKey Structure\n```typescript\nexport type InstanceSessionKey = {\n  _type: TypeRef<InstanceSessionKey>;\n  _id: Id;\n  instanceId: Id;           // The ID of the entity (e.g., MailDetailsBlob ID)\n  instanceList: Id;         // The list containing the instance\n  symEncSessionKey: Uint8Array;  // The encrypted session key\n  typeInfo: TypeInfo;       // Type information\n}\n```\n\n**Session Key Cache** (`/app/src/api/worker/crypto/CryptoFacade.ts`, lines 80-84):\n\n```typescript\nexport class CryptoFacade {\n  // Caches session keys by element ID to optimize performance\n  private readonly sessionKeyCache: Record<string, Aes128Key> = {}\n  \n  // Used for Mail and MailBody (they share the same session key)\n  // Also optimizes performance when loading MailDetails\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 3. Entity Loading and Decryption\n\n**EntityRestClient Flow** (`/app/src/api/worker/rest/EntityRestClient.ts`, lines 114-147):\n\n1. **Load from server** (HTTP GET)\n2. **Apply migrations** (handle schema changes)\n3. **Resolve session key** using one of these strategies:\n   - From cache (if already loaded)\n   - From bucketKey (new permission model)\n   - From _ownerEncSessionKey (if user is in owner group)\n   - From Permission objects (legacy public/external permissions)\n4. **Decrypt and map** to instance using InstanceMapper\n5. **Cache** session key for related entities\n\n**Session Key Resolution Hierarchy** (`/app/src/api/worker/crypto/CryptoFacade.ts`, lines 193-250):\n\n```typescript\nresolveSessionKey(typeModel: TypeModel, instance: Record<string, any>): Promise<Aes128Key | null> {\n  1. Check sessionKeyCache\n  2. If bucketKey exists:\n     - Decrypt bucketKey\n     - Extract appropriate session key for this instance\n  3. Else if _ownerEncSessionKey exists AND user is in ownerGroup:\n     - Decrypt with owner group key\n  4. Else if ownerEncSessionKey exists (service instances):\n     - Decrypt with mail group key\n  5. Else:\n     - Load Permission entities\n     - Try symmetric permission first\n     - Fall back to public/external permission with BucketPermission\n}\n```\n\n**InstanceMapper Decryption** (`/app/src/api/worker/crypto/InstanceMapper.ts`, lines 24-83):\n\n- Iterates through all model values\n- Decrypts each encrypted field using the session key\n- Handles aggregations recursively\n- Stores encrypted values for later updates (_finalEncrypted_ and _defaultEncrypted_)\n\n---\n\n## 4. Legacy vs. Non-Legacy Permission Models\n\n**Identification** (`/app/src/api/common/MailWrapper.ts`, lines 110-116):\n\n```typescript\nexport function isLegacyMail(mail: Mail): boolean {\n  return mail.mailDetails == null && mail.mailDetailsDraft == null\n}\n\nexport function isDetailsDraft(mail: Mail): boolean {\n  return mail.mailDetailsDraft != null\n}\n```\n\n### Legacy Model encrypted with same key as Mail\n\n### New Model Characteristics:\n- Mail contains `bucketKey: BucketKey` (contains session keys for multiple entities)\n- Mail contains `mailDetails: IdTuple` or instance, typeModel))\n```\n\n---\n\n## 5. {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01QzfUd1uBWm1Y9tcTFoNKGY","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_016tTooe1hX5m34CCBFvTDu7","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/BUG_ANALYSIS.md","content":"# Bug Analysis: Non-legacy Mail Content Fails to Decrypt\n\n## Summary\nNon-legacy mails in Tutanota fail to decrypt due to missing session key propagation when loading related entities (MailDetailsBlob, MailDetailsDraft). Users experience blank message bodies, missing reply-to addresses, and failed mail indexing.\n\n## Root Cause\n\n### The Architecture\n- **Legacy mails**: Store body directly on Mail entity, use `_ownerEncSessionKey` for encryption\n- **Non-legacy mails**: Store body in MailDetailsBlob/MailDetailsDraft, use `bucketKey` to manage session keys for multiple entities\n\n### The Bug\nIn `CryptoFacade.resolveSessionKey()` (app/src/api/worker/crypto/CryptoFacade.ts, lines 193-250):\n\n```typescript\n// Session key caching happens AFTER the function returns\n.then((sessionKey) => {\n    if (sessionKey && isSameTypeRefByAttr(MailTypeRef, typeModel.app, typeModel.name)) {\n        if (this.isTuple(instance.mailDetails)) {\n            this.setSessionKeyCacheWithTuple(instance.mailDetails, sessionKey)  // Cache set here\n        }\n    }\n    return sessionKey\n})\n```\n\n### The Timing Issue\n1. **Mail loading**: `resolveSessionKey(Mail)` returns and session key is extracted from bucketKey ✓\n2. **Cache update**: `.then()` handler executes and caches session key for MailDetailsBlob ID\n3. **Details loading**: `loadMailDetails()` calls `entityClient.loadMultiple()` immediately\n4. **Problem**: `resolveSessionKey(MailDetailsBlob)` runs BEFORE cache is populated\n5. **Result**: \"could not resolve session key\" error for MailDetailsBlob\n\n### Where It Fails\n\n#### Path 1: Direct Load (loadMailDetails - non-draft)\n```\nloadMailDetails(mail)\n  └─ entityClient.loadMultiple(MailDetailsBlobTypeRef, ...)  // Loads immediately\n      └─ resolveSessionKey(MailDetailsBlob)  // Cache NOT populated yet ✗\n          └─ throws SessionKeyNotFoundError\n```\n\n#### Path 2: Batch Load (Multiple entities)\nWhen `loadMultiple()` is called with multiple entity IDs:\n- Session keys in bucketKey are not forwarded to the decryption layer\n- Each entity fails independently to resolve its session key\n\n#### Path 3: Mail Indexer\nMail indexer tries to index non-legacy mails:\n- Calls `loadMailDetails()` for each mail\n- Session key propagation fails\n- Indexing fails silently with decryption errors\n\n## Symptoms\n\n1. **Blank mail bodies**: Mail body text cannot be decrypted, users see empty message\n2. **Missing reply-to addresses**: Stored in MailDetails, cannot be decrypted\n3. **Failed mail indexing**: Search/indexer encounters non-legacy mails but fails silently\n4. **Console errors**: \"Missing decryption key\" / \"could not resolve session key\"\n\n## Code Flow\n\n### In `MailUtils.ts` (lines 397-408)\n```typescript\nexport async function loadMailDetails(entityClient: EntityClient, mail: Mail): Promise<MailWrapper> {\n    // For non-legacy mails:\n    const mailDetailsId = neverNull(mail.mailDetails)\n    return entityClient\n        .loadMultiple(MailDetailsBlobTypeRef, listIdPart(mailDetailsId), [elementIdPart(mailDetailsId)])\n        .then((d) => MailWrapper.details(mail, d[0].details))\n\n    // BUG: mail object with bucketKey is available but not passed to loadMultiple()\n    // The session key is never explicitly provided to the load operation\n}\n```\n\n### In `EntityRestClient.ts` (lines 114-147)\n```typescript\nasync load<T extends SomeEntity>(\n    typeRef: TypeRef<T>,\n    id: ...,\n    ...,\n    ownerKey?: Aes128Key,  // Session key can be passed here\n): Promise<T> {\n    // But loadMailDetails() never uses this parameter\n    const sessionKey = ownerKey\n        ? this.resolveSessionKeyWithOwnerKey(...)\n        : await this.resolveSessionKey(...)  // Tries to resolve from cache/permissions\n}\n```\n\n## The Fix Would Require\n\n1. **Extract session key from Mail's bucketKey** before calling `loadMultiple()`\n2. **Pre-populate cache** with all session keys from bucketKey before loading details\n3. OR **Pass session keys explicitly** to `loadMultiple()` (requires API changes)\n4. OR **Ensure cache is populated synchronously** before loading details\n\n## Test Coverage\n\nThe regression test (`regression_test.test.ts`) demonstrates:\n\n1. ✓ Session key not available when loading MailDetailsBlob\n2. ✓ Blank mail body due to decryption failure\n3. ✓ Reply-to addresses cannot be decrypted\n4. ✓ Batch loading fails for multiple non-legacy mails\n5. ✓ Mail indexer fails silently with non-legacy mails\n6. ✓ Exact code path where session key caching timing fails\n\n## Files Involved\n\n- `app/src/api/worker/crypto/CryptoFacade.ts` - Session key resolution logic\n- `app/src/mail/model/MailUtils.ts` - Mail details loading\n- `app/src/api/worker/rest/EntityRestClient.ts` - Entity loading and caching\n- `app/src/api/worker/crypto/InstanceMapper.ts` - Decryption and error handling\n- `app/src/api/common/MailWrapper.ts` - Legacy vs non-legacy mail detection\n- `app/src/api/entities/tutanota/TypeRefs.ts` - Mail and MailDetailsBlob definitions\n- `app/src/api/entities/sys/TypeRefs.ts` - BucketKey and InstanceSessionKey definitions\n\n## Key Code Locations\n\n| Issue | File | Lines |\n|-------|------|-------|\n| Session key caching timing | `CryptoFacade.ts` | 231-242 |\n| Cache lookup | `CryptoFacade.ts` | 200-212 |\n| BucketKey resolution | `CryptoFacade.ts` | 212-216 |\n| loadMailDetails() | `MailUtils.ts` | 397-408 |\n| Entity loading | `EntityRestClient.ts` | 173-180 |\n| Decryption error handling | `InstanceMapper.ts` | 33-42 |\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":0,"cache_creation_input_tokens":229,"cache_read_input_tokens":71373,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":229},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"bbc63886-0484-4394-a0f8-9a397a86e990","uuid":"2905ced9-7bd8-4658-85f8-3311b9a5b8cb"}
